\doxysubsection{Detailed Description}
The Ginkgo namespace. 

\doxysubsection{Typedef Documentation}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacegko_a6837b759dc528737540a83c79fbdda29}\label{namespacegko_a6837b759dc528737540a83c79fbdda29}} 
\index{gko@{gko}!highest\_precision@{highest\_precision}}
\index{highest\_precision@{highest\_precision}!gko@{gko}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{highest\_precision}{highest\_precision}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$typename... Ts$>$ \\
using \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacegko_a6837b759dc528737540a83c79fbdda29}{gko\+::highest\+\_\+precision}} = typedef typename detail\+::highest\+\_\+precision\+\_\+variadic$<$Ts...$>$\+::type}



Obtains the smallest arithmetic type that is able to store elements of all template parameter types exactly. 

All template type parameters need to be either real or complex types, mixing them is not possible.

Formally, it computes a right-\/fold over the type list, with the highest precision of a pair of real arithmetic types T1, T2 computed as {\ttfamily decltype(T1\{\} + T2\{\})}, or {\ttfamily std\+::complex$<$highest\+\_\+precision$<$remove\+\_\+complex$<$T1$>$, remove\+\_\+complex$<$T2$>$$>$$>$} for complex types. \mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacegko_a7a3f195040a356643b3e8659554c7a48}\label{namespacegko_a7a3f195040a356643b3e8659554c7a48}} 
\index{gko@{gko}!is\_complex\_or\_scalar\_s@{is\_complex\_or\_scalar\_s}}
\index{is\_complex\_or\_scalar\_s@{is\_complex\_or\_scalar\_s}!gko@{gko}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{is\_complex\_or\_scalar\_s}{is\_complex\_or\_scalar\_s}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$typename T $>$ \\
using \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacegko_a7a3f195040a356643b3e8659554c7a48}{gko\+::is\+\_\+complex\+\_\+or\+\_\+scalar\+\_\+s}} = typedef detail\+::is\+\_\+complex\+\_\+or\+\_\+scalar\+\_\+impl$<$T$>$}



Allows to check if T is a complex or scalar value during compile time by accessing the {\ttfamily value} attribute of this struct. 

If {\ttfamily value} is {\ttfamily true}, T is a complex/scalar type, if it is {\ttfamily false}, T is not a complex/scalar type.

\doxysubsection{Enumeration Type Documentation}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacegko_afbed8e2cbd3ee4ca962e12f688858bdb}\label{namespacegko_afbed8e2cbd3ee4ca962e12f688858bdb}} 
\index{gko@{gko}!allocation\_mode@{allocation\_mode}}
\index{allocation\_mode@{allocation\_mode}!gko@{gko}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{allocation\_mode}{allocation\_mode}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily enum \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacegko_afbed8e2cbd3ee4ca962e12f688858bdb}{gko\+::allocation\+\_\+mode}}\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [strong]}}



Specify the mode of allocation for C\+U\+D\+A/\+H\+IP G\+P\+Us. 

{\ttfamily device} allocates memory on the device and Unified Memory model is not used.

{\ttfamily unified\+\_\+global} allocates memory on the device, but is accessible by the host through the Unified memory model.

{\ttfamily unified\+\_\+host} allocates memory on the host and it is not available on devices which do not have concurrent accesses switched on, but this access can be explicitly switched on, when necessary. \mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacegko_ae749a5ea11a93c1bcc9158d9a6e9fb68}\label{namespacegko_ae749a5ea11a93c1bcc9158d9a6e9fb68}} 
\index{gko@{gko}!layout\_type@{layout\_type}}

Specifies the layout type when writing data in matrix market format.

Referenced by gko\+::\+Scaled\+Identity\+Addable\+::add\+\_\+scaled\+\_\+identity(), gko\+::\+Lin\+Op\+::apply(), gko\+::matrix\+::\+Csr$<$ Value\+Type, Index\+Type $>$\+::inv\+\_\+scale(), and gko\+::matrix\+::\+Csr$<$ Value\+Type, Index\+Type $>$\+::scale().

\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacegko_ad1f2b88f3b91582e67c7c6d8730300a2}\label{namespacegko_ad1f2b88f3b91582e67c7c6d8730300a2}} 
\index{gko@{gko}!make\_temporary\_conversion@{make\_temporary\_conversion}}
\index{make\_temporary\_conversion@{make\_temporary\_conversion}!gko@{gko}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{make\_temporary\_conversion()}{make\_temporary\_conversion()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$typename Value\+Type , typename Ptr $>$ \\
detail\+::temporary\+\_\+conversion$<$std\+::conditional\+\_\+t$<$ std\+::is\+\_\+const$<$detail\+::pointee$<$Ptr$>$ $>$\+::value, const \mbox{\hyperlink{classgko_1_1matrix_1_1Dense}{matrix\+::\+Dense}}$<$Value\+Type$>$, \mbox{\hyperlink{classgko_1_1matrix_1_1Dense}{matrix\+::\+Dense}}$<$Value\+Type$>$ $>$ $>$ gko\+::make\+\_\+temporary\+\_\+conversion (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Ptr \&\&}]{matrix }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Convert the given \mbox{\hyperlink{classgko_1_1LinOp}{Lin\+Op}} from matrix\+::\+Dense$<$...$>$ to matrix\+::\+Dense$<$\+Value\+Type$>$. 

The conversion tries to convert the input \mbox{\hyperlink{classgko_1_1LinOp}{Lin\+Op}} to all Dense types with value type recursively reachable by next\+\_\+precision$<$...$>$ starting from the Value\+Type template parameter. This means that all real-\/to-\/real and complex-\/to-\/complex conversions for default precisions are being considered. If the input matrix is non-\/const, the contents of the modified converted object will be converted back to the input matrix when the returned object is destroyed. This may lead to a loss of precision!


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em matrix} & the input matrix which is supposed to be converted. It is wrapped unchanged if it is already of type matrix\+::\+Dense$<$\+Value\+Type$>$, otherwise it will be converted to this type if possible.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
a detail\+::temporary\+\_\+conversion pointing to the (potentially converted) object.
\end{DoxyReturn}

\begin{DoxyExceptions}{Exceptions}
{\em \mbox{\hyperlink{classgko_1_1NotSupported}{Not\+Supported}}} & if the input matrix cannot be converted to matrix\+::\+Dense$<$\+Value\+Type$>$\\
\hline
\end{DoxyExceptions}

\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{Template Parameters}
{\em Value\+Type} & the value type into whose associated \mbox{\hyperlink{classgko_1_1matrix_1_1Dense}{matrix\+::\+Dense}} type to convert the input \mbox{\hyperlink{classgko_1_1LinOp}{Lin\+Op}}. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacegko_a5bb0c29332dae13bf6aa8771583d7b06}\label{namespacegko_a5bb0c29332dae13bf6aa8771583d7b06}} 
\index{gko@{gko}!make\_temporary\_output\_clone@{make\_temporary\_output\_clone}}
\index{make\_temporary\_output\_clone@{make\_temporary\_output\_clone}!gko@{gko}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{make\_temporary\_output\_clone()}{make\_temporary\_output\_clone()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$typename Ptr $>$ \\
detail\+::temporary\+\_\+clone$<$detail\+::pointee$<$Ptr$>$ $>$ gko\+::make\+\_\+temporary\+\_\+output\+\_\+clone (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{std\+::shared\+\_\+ptr$<$ const \mbox{\hyperlink{classgko_1_1Executor}{Executor}} $>$}]{exec,  }\item[{Ptr \&\&}]{ptr }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Creates a uninitialized temporary\+\_\+clone that will be copied back to the input afterwards. 

It can be used for output parameters to avoid an unnecessary copy in make\+\_\+temporary\+\_\+clone.

This is a helper function which avoids the need to explicitly specify the type of the object, as would be the case if using the constructor of temporary\+\_\+clone.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em exec} & the executor where the uninitialized clone will be created \\
\hline
{\em ptr} & a pointer to the object of which the clone will be created\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{Template Parameters}
{\em Ptr} & the (raw or smart) pointer type to be temporarily cloned \\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacegko_a205901dcce27e1df970c569d46d87551}\label{namespacegko_a205901dcce27e1df970c569d46d87551}} 
\index{gko@{gko}!mixed\_precision\_dispatch@{mixed\_precision\_dispatch}}
\index{mixed\_precision\_dispatch@{mixed\_precision\_dispatch}!gko@{gko}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{mixed\_precision\_dispatch()}{mixed\_precision\_dispatch()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$typename Value\+Type , typename Function $>$ \\
void gko\+::mixed\+\_\+precision\+\_\+dispatch (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Function}]{fn,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classgko_1_1LinOp}{Lin\+Op}} $\ast$}]{in,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classgko_1_1LinOp}{Lin\+Op}} $\ast$}]{out }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Calls the given function with each given argument \mbox{\hyperlink{classgko_1_1LinOp}{Lin\+Op}} converted into matrix\+::\+Dense$<$\+Value\+Type$>$ as parameters. 

If G\+I\+N\+K\+G\+O\+\_\+\+M\+I\+X\+E\+D\+\_\+\+P\+R\+E\+C\+I\+S\+I\+ON is defined, this means that the function will be called with its dynamic type as a static type, so the (templated/generic) function will be instantiated with all pairs of Dense$<$\+Value\+Type$>$ and Dense$<$next\+\_\+precision$<$\+Value\+Type$>$$>$ parameter types, and the appropriate overload will be called based on the dynamic type of the parameter.

If G\+I\+N\+K\+G\+O\+\_\+\+M\+I\+X\+E\+D\+\_\+\+P\+R\+E\+C\+I\+S\+I\+ON is not defined, it will behave exactly like precision\+\_\+dispatch.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em fn} & the given function. It will be called with one const and one non-\/const matrix\+::\+Dense$<$...$>$ parameter based on the dynamic type of the inputs (G\+I\+N\+K\+G\+O\+\_\+\+M\+I\+X\+E\+D\+\_\+\+P\+R\+E\+C\+I\+S\+I\+ON) or of type matrix\+::\+Dense$<$\+Value\+Type$>$ (no G\+I\+N\+K\+G\+O\+\_\+\+M\+I\+X\+E\+D\+\_\+\+P\+R\+E\+C\+I\+S\+I\+ON). \\
\hline
{\em in} & The first parameter to be cast (G\+I\+N\+K\+G\+O\+\_\+\+M\+I\+X\+E\+D\+\_\+\+P\+R\+E\+C\+I\+S\+I\+ON) or converted (no G\+I\+N\+K\+G\+O\+\_\+\+M\+I\+X\+E\+D\+\_\+\+P\+R\+E\+C\+I\+S\+I\+ON) and used to call {\ttfamily fn}. \\
\hline
{\em out} & The second parameter to be cast (G\+I\+N\+K\+G\+O\+\_\+\+M\+I\+X\+E\+D\+\_\+\+P\+R\+E\+C\+I\+S\+I\+ON) or converted (no G\+I\+N\+K\+G\+O\+\_\+\+M\+I\+X\+E\+D\+\_\+\+P\+R\+E\+C\+I\+S\+I\+ON) and used to call {\ttfamily fn}.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{Template Parameters}
{\em Value\+Type} & the value type to use for the parameters of {\ttfamily fn} (no G\+I\+N\+K\+G\+O\+\_\+\+M\+I\+X\+E\+D\+\_\+\+P\+R\+E\+C\+I\+S\+I\+ON). With G\+I\+N\+K\+G\+O\+\_\+\+M\+I\+X\+E\+D\+\_\+\+P\+R\+E\+C\+I\+S\+I\+ON enabled, it only matters whether this type is complex or real. \\
\hline
{\em Function} & the function pointer, lambda or other functor type to call with the converted arguments. \\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}
\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacegko_a3b9785eed86179e15b8fb4e74f7e9f89}\label{namespacegko_a3b9785eed86179e15b8fb4e74f7e9f89}} 
\index{gko@{gko}!mixed\_precision\_dispatch\_real\_complex@{mixed\_precision\_dispatch\_real\_complex}}
\index{mixed\_precision\_dispatch\_real\_complex@{mixed\_precision\_dispatch\_real\_complex}!gko@{gko}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{mixed\_precision\_dispatch\_real\_complex()}{mixed\_precision\_dispatch\_real\_complex()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$typename Value\+Type , typename Function , std\+::enable\+\_\+if\+\_\+t$<$ is\+\_\+complex$<$ Value\+Type $>$()$>$ $\ast$  = nullptr$>$ \\
void gko\+::mixed\+\_\+precision\+\_\+dispatch\+\_\+real\+\_\+complex (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Function}]{fn,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classgko_1_1LinOp}{Lin\+Op}} $\ast$}]{in,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classgko_1_1LinOp}{Lin\+Op}} $\ast$}]{out }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Calls the given function with the given Lin\+Ops cast to their dynamic type matrix\+::\+Dense$<$\+Value\+Type$>$$\ast$ as parameters. 

If Value\+Type is real and both {\ttfamily in} and {\ttfamily out} are complex, uses matrix\+::\+Dense\+::get\+\_\+real\+\_\+view() to convert them into real matrices after precision conversion.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$typename Value\+Type , typename Function , typename... Args$>$ \\
void gko\+::precision\+\_\+dispatch (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Function}]{fn,  }\item[{Args $\ast$...}]{linops }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Calls the given function with each given argument \mbox{\hyperlink{classgko_1_1LinOp}{Lin\+Op}} temporarily converted into matrix\+::\+Dense$<$\+Value\+Type$>$ as parameters. 


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em fn} & the given function. It will be passed one (potentially const) matrix\+::\+Dense$<$\+Value\+Type$>$$\ast$ parameter per parameter in the parameter pack {\ttfamily linops}. \\
\hline

\end{DoxyParams}

\hline

{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$typename Value\+Type , typename Function $>$ \\
void gko\+::precision\+\_\+dispatch\+\_\+real\+\_\+complex (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Function}]{fn,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classgko_1_1LinOp}{Lin\+Op}} $\ast$}]{alpha,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classgko_1_1LinOp}{Lin\+Op}} $\ast$}]{in,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classgko_1_1LinOp}{Lin\+Op}} $\ast$}]{beta,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classgko_1_1LinOp}{Lin\+Op}} $\ast$}]{out }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Calls the given function with the given Lin\+Ops temporarily converted to matrix\+::\+Dense$<$\+Value\+Type$>$$\ast$ as parameters. 

If Value\+Type is real and both {\ttfamily in} and {\ttfamily out} are complex, uses matrix\+::\+Dense\+::get\+\_\+real\+\_\+view() to convert them into real matrices after precision conversion.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$typename Value\+Type , typename Function $>$ \\
void gko\+::precision\+\_\+dispatch\+\_\+real\+\_\+complex (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Function}]{fn,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classgko_1_1LinOp}{Lin\+Op}} $\ast$}]{alpha,  }\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{classgko_1_1LinOp}{Lin\+Op}} $\ast$}]{in,  }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classgko_1_1LinOp}{Lin\+Op}} $\ast$}]{out }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Calls the given function with the given Lin\+Ops temporarily converted to matrix\+::\+Dense$<$\+Value\+Type$>$$\ast$ as parameters. 

If Value\+Type is real and both {\ttfamily in} and {\ttfamily out} are complex, uses matrix\+::\+Dense\+::get\+\_\+real\+\_\+view() to convert them into real matrices after precision conversion.

References read\+\_\+binary\+\_\+raw().

\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacegko_a4c57f7b636344e8b4d17d42d2f17358f}\label{namespacegko_a4c57f7b636344e8b4d17d42d2f17358f}} 
\index{gko@{gko}!read\_binary\_raw@{read\_binary\_raw}}
\index{read\_binary\_raw@{read\_binary\_raw}!gko@{gko}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{read\_binary\_raw()}{read\_binary\_raw()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$typename Value\+Type  = default\+\_\+precision, typename Index\+Type  = int32$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{structgko_1_1matrix__data}{matrix\+\_\+data}}$<$Value\+Type, Index\+Type$>$ gko\+::read\+\_\+binary\+\_\+raw (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{std\+::istream \&}]{is }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Reads a matrix stored in Ginkgo\textquotesingle{}s binary matrix format from an input stream. 

Note that this format depends on the processor\textquotesingle{}s endianness, so files from a big endian processor can\textquotesingle{}t be read from a little endian processor and vice-\/versa.

The binary format has the following structure (in system endianness)\+:
\begin{DoxyEnumerate}
\item A 32 byte header consisting of 4 uint64\+\_\+t values\+: magic = G\+I\+N\+K\+G\+O\+\_\+\+\_\+\+: The highest two bytes stand for value and index type. value type\+: S (float), D (double), C (complex$<$float$>$), Z(complex$<$double$>$) index type\+: I (int32), L (int64) num\+\_\+rows\+: Number of rows num\+\_\+cols\+: Number of columns num\+\_\+entries\+: Number of (row, column, value) tuples to follow
\item Following are num\+\_\+entries blocks of size sizeof(\+Index\+Type) $\ast$ 2 + sizeof(\+Value\+Type). Each consists of a row index stored as Index\+Type, followed by a column index stored as Index\+Type and a value stored as Value\+Type.
\end{DoxyEnumerate}


\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{Template Parameters}
{\em Value\+Type} & type of matrix values \\
\hline
{\em Index\+Type} & type of matrix indexes\\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em is} & input stream from which to read the data\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A \mbox{\hyperlink{structgko_1_1matrix__data}{matrix\+\_\+data}} structure containing the matrix. The nonzero elements are sorted in lexicographic order of their (row, column) indexes.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
This is an advanced routine that will return the raw matrix data structure. Consider using \mbox{\hyperlink{namespacegko_ad10dc71f76a4125568cb0ab5add863cd}{gko\+::read\+\_\+binary}} instead. 
\end{DoxyNote}


Referenced by read\+\_\+binary().

References one().

\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespacegko_a537803d962d07cf43e1e0cbc9f6a3f8b}\label{namespacegko_a537803d962d07cf43e1e0cbc9f6a3f8b}} 
\index{gko@{gko}!with\_matrix\_type@{with\_matrix\_type}}
\index{with\_matrix\_type@{with\_matrix\_type}!gko@{gko}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{with\_matrix\_type()}{with\_matrix\_type()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily template$<$template$<$ typename, typename $>$ class Matrix\+Type, typename... Args$>$ \\
auto gko\+::with\+\_\+matrix\+\_\+type (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Args \&\&...}]{create\+\_\+args }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



This function returns a type that delays a call to Matrix\+Type\+::create. 

It can be used to set the used value and index type, as well as the executor at a later stage.

For example, the following code creates first a temporary object, which is then used later to construct an operator of the previously defined base type\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{auto} type = gko::with\_matrix\_type<gko::matrix::Csr>();}
\DoxyCodeLine{...}
\DoxyCodeLine{std::unique\_ptr<LinOp> concrete\_op}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keywordflow}{if}(flag1)\{}
\DoxyCodeLine{  concrete\_op = type.template create<double, int>(exec);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\} \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{  concrete\_op = type.template create<float, int>(exec);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\}}
\end{DoxyCode}


\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
This is mainly a helper function to specify the local matrix type for a \mbox{\hyperlink{classgko_1_1experimental_1_1distributed_1_1Matrix}{gko\+::experimental\+::distributed\+::\+Matrix}} more easily.
\end{DoxyNote}

\begin{DoxyTemplParams}{Template Parameters}
{\em Matrix\+Type} & A template type that accepts two types, the first one will be set to the value type, the second one to the index type. \\
\hline
{\em Args} & Types of the arguments passed to Matrix\+Type\+::create.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyTemplParams}

\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em create\+\_\+args} & arguments that will be forwarded to Matrix\+Type\+::create\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A type with a function {\ttfamily create$<$value\+\_\+type, index\+\_\+type$>$(executor)}. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

Writes a matrix into an output stream in binary format. 

Note that this format depends on the processor\textquotesingle{}s endianness, so files from a big endian processor can\textquotesingle{}t be read from a little endian processor and vice-\/versa.
